 upasaṅkamma samubuddhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 vanditvā satthuno pāde imaṃ vacanamabraviṃ  
  
       navasassaṃ ca sampannaṃ āyāgo pi  ca tvaṃ mune  
 anukampamupādāya adhivāsehi cakkhuma  
  
       padumuttaro lokavidū āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho  
 mama saṅkappamaññāya imaṃ  vacanamabravi  
  
       cattāro ca paṭipannā cattāro ca phale ṭhitā  
 esa saṅgho ujubhūto paññāsīlasamāhito  
  
       yajantānaṃ manussānaṃ puññapekkhānapāṇinaṃ  
 karotopadhikaṃ puññaṃ saṅghe dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ  
  
    phalinaṃ  machasaṃ  
    dhaññamāritvā  sīmu  
    āyāgosi  machasaṃ  idhahosi  syā  
    idaṃ  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       tasmiṃ saṅghe padātabbaṃ  navasassaṃ  tathetaraṃ  
 saṅghato uddisitvāna bhikkhū tetvāna saṃgharaṃ  
 paṭiyattaṃ ghare yantaṃ  bhikkhusaṅghassa dehi tvaṃ   
  
       saṅghato uddisitvāna bhikkhu netvānahaṃ gharaṃ  
 yaṃ ghare paṭiyattaṃ me bhikkhusaṅghassadāsahaṃ  
  
       tena kammena sukatena cetanā paṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ  
  
       tattha me sukataṃ vyamhaṃ sovaṇṇaṃ sappabhassaraṃ  
 saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ  
  
  ekūnavīsatimaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ    
  
       ākiṇṇaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ nārigaṇasamākulaṃ  
 tattha bhutvā pivitvā ca vasāmi tidase ahaṃ  
  
       satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuṃ ca devarajjamakārayiṃ  
 satānaṃ piñcakkhattuṃ ca cakkavatti ahosahaṃ  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyo  
  
       bhavābhave              saṃsaranto labhāmi amitaṃ dhanaṃ  
 bhoge me ūnatā natthi navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ sivikaṃ sandamānikaṃ  
 labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       navavatthaṃ navaphalaṃ navaggarasabhojanaṃ  
 labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       koseyyakambaliyāni khomakappāsikāni ca  
 labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       dāsīgaṇaṃ dāsagaṇaṃ nāriyo ca alaṅkatā  
 labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       na maṃ sītaṃ vā uṇhaṃ vā pariḷāho na vijjati  
 atho cetasikaṃ dukkhaṃ hadaye me na vijjati  
  
       imaṃ khāda imaṃ bhuñja imamhi sayane saya  
 labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
    saṅghedātabbaṃ  machasaṃ  saṅghe ca dātabbaṃ syā      
    tava sassaṃ  machasaṃ  
    santaṃ  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       ayaṃ pacchimakodāni carimo vattane bhavo  
 ajjāpi deyyadhammo  me phalaṃ toseti sabbadā  
  
       navasassaṃ daditvāna saṅghe gaṇavaruttame  
 aṭṭhānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama  
  
       vaṇṇavā yasavā homi mahābhogo anītiko  
 mahesakkho  sadā homi abhejjapariso sadā  
  
       sabbe maṃ apavāyanti ye keci paṭhavissitā  
 deyyadhammā ca ye keci pure pure labhāmahaṃ  
  
       bhikkhusaṅghassa vā majjhe buddhaseṭṭhassa sammukhā  
 sabbepi samatikkamma denti mayheva  dāyakā  
  
       paṭhamaṃ navasassaṃ hi datvā saṅghe gaṇuttame  
 imānisaṃse anubhomi navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sucintito thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 sucintitattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ  
  
      soṇṇakiṅkaṇiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       saddhāya              abhinikkhamma pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ  
 vākacīradharo āsiṃ tapokammamapassito  
  
       atthadassī tu bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 upapajji tamhi samaye tārayanto mahājanaṃ  
  
    deyyadhamme  sīmu  
    mahāsakkho  syā  
    mameva  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       balañca vata me khīṇaṃ vyādhinā paramena tu  
 buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna pulite thūpamuttamaṃ 
  
       karitvā haṭṭhavittohaṃ sahatthena samokiriṃ  
 soṇṇakiṅkaṇipupphāni udaggamanaso ahaṃ  
  
       sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ phūpaṃ parivariṃ ahaṃ  
 tena cetopasādena atthidassissa tādino  
  
       devalokaṃ gato santo labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ  
 suvaṇṇavaṇṇo tatthāsiṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       asītikoṭiyo mayhaṃ nāriyo samalaṅkatā  
 sadā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhanti buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       saṭṭhituriyasahassāni bheriyo paṇavāni ca  
 saṅkhā ca deṇḍimā  tattha vagguṃ nadanti  dunduhi  
  
       cullāsītisahassāni hatthino samalaṅkatā  
 tidhāpabhinnamātaṅgā kuñjarā saṭṭhīhāyanā  
  
       hemajālāhi sañchannā upaṭṭhānaṃ karonti me  
 balakāye gaje ceva ūnatā me ne vijjati  
  
       soṇṇakiṅkaṇipupphānaṃ cakkavatti ahosahaṃ  
 pathavyārajjaṃ ekasataṃ mahiyā kārayiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       ekasattatikkhattuñca cakkavatti ahosahaṃ  
 pathavyārajjaṃ ekasataṃ mahiyā kārayiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       sodāni patto amataṃ  asaṅkhataṃ sududdasaṃ    
 saṃyojanaparikkhīṇo natthidāni punabbhavo  
  
       aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ pupphambhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā              jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasesā ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sovaṇṇakiṅkaṇiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 sovaṇṇakiṅkaṇiyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ  
  
    ḍiṇḍimā  machasaṃ  
    vagguvajjanti  machasaṃ  
    amataṃ patto  machasaṃ  
    gambhīraṃ draddasaṃ padaṃ  syā  
  
               
  
      soṇṇanakontarikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       manobhāvanīyaṃ buddhaṃ attadantaṃ samāhitaṃ  
 irīyamānaṃ brahmapathe cittavūpasame rataṃ  
  
       nittiṇṇaoghaṃ sambuddhaṃ jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ muniṃ  
 upaviṭṭhaṃ samāpannaṃ indīvaradalappabhaṃ  
  
       alābunodakaṃ gayha buddhaseṭṭhamupāgamiṃ  
 buddhassa pāde dhovitvā alābudakamadāsahaṃ  
  
       āṇāpesi ca sambuddho padumuttaranāyako  
 iminā dakamāhatvā  pādamūle ṭhapehi me  
  
       sādhūtihaṃ paṭissutvā satthugāravatāya ca  
 dakaṃ alābunāhitvā  buddhaseṭṭhamupānayiṃ  
  
       anumodi mahāvīro cittaṃ nibbāpayaṃ mama  
 iminā lābudānena saṅkappo te samijjhatu  
  
       paṇṇarasasu kappesu devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ  
 tiṃsatikkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti ahosahaṃ  
  
       divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ caṅkamantassa tiṭṭhato  
 sovaṇṇakontaraṃ gayha tiṭṭhate  purato mama  
  
       buddhassa lābuṃ datvāna  labhāmi soṇṇakontaraṃ  
 appakampi kataṃ kāraṃ vipulaṃ hoti tādisu  
  
       satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ lābumadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi alābussa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā soṇṇakontariko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 soṇṇakontarikattherassa              apadānaṃ dasamaṃ  
  
    imino dakamāhatvā  sīmu  
    alābunābhitvā  sīmu  
    tiṭṭhanti  sīmu 
    datvāna lābu  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
 uddānaṃ  
  
 sakiṃsammajjako thero ekadussī ekāsanī  
 kadambakoraṇḍakadā  ghataṃ savaṇiko  pi ca  
  
 sucintito kiṅkaṇiko soṇṇakontariko pi ca  
 ekaṃ gāthāsatañceva  ekasattatimeva ca  
  
 sakiṃsammajjakavaggo tevattāḷisamo  
  
      ekavihāriyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso  
 kassapo nāma gottena uppajji vadataṃ varo  
  
       nippapañco nirālambo ākāsasamamānaso  
 suññatābahulo tādī animittarato vasī  
  
       asaṅgacitto nikleso  asaṃsaṭṭho kule gaṇe  
 mahākāruṇiko vīro vinayopāyakovido  
  
       uyyutto parakiccesu vinayanto sadevake  
 nibbānagamanaṃ maggaṃ gati paṅkavisosanaṃ  
  
       amataṃ paramassādaṃ  jarāmaccunivāraṇaṃ  
 mahāparisamajjhe so nisinno lokatāraṇo   
  
       karavīkaruto  nātho brahmaghoso tathāgato  
 uddharanto mahāduggā vipannaddhe  anāyake  
  
       desento virajaṃ dhammaṃ diṭṭho me lokanāyako  
 tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāna pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ  
  
       pabbajitvā tadā cāhaṃ   cintento jinasāsanaṃ  
 ekakova vane ramme vasiṃ saṃsaggapīḷito  
       sakāyavupakasso   me hetubhuto mahābhavi    
 manaso vūpakassassa   saṃsaggahayadassino  
  
       kilesā              jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
    kadambakoraṇḍakado  machasaṃ  
    ghatassavanikopica  machasaṃ  
    ekagāthā satañcettha  machasaṃ  
    nillepo  syā  
    gatiṃ  machasaṃ  
    paramassāsaṃ  sīmu  
    lokatārako  machasaṃ  
    karavikarudo  syā  
    vippanaṭṭho  sīmu  machasaṃ  
     pāhaṃ  machasaṃ  
    sakkāyavūpakāso  machasaṃ  
     mamāgamī  syā      
     vūpakāsassa  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasesā ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhīme  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekavihāriyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 ekavihāriyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ  
  
      ekasaṃkhiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       vipassino bhagavato mahābodhimaho ahu  
 mahājanā samāgamma pūjenti bodhimuttamaṃ  
  
       na hi taṃ orakaṃ maññe buddhaseṭṭho bhavissati  
 yassāyamediso  bodhi pūjanīyo  ca satthuno  
  
       tato saṅkhaṃ gahetvāna bodhirukkhaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ    
 dhamento sabbadivasaṃ avandiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ  
  
       āsannake kataṃ kammaṃ devalokaṃ apāpayī  
 kaḷebaraṃ me patitaṃ devaloke ramāmahaṃ  
  
       saṭṭhituriyasahassāni tuṭṭhahaṭṭhā pamoditā  
 sadā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhanti buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ekasattatime kappe rājā āsiṃ sudassano  
 cāturanto vijitāvī jambusaṇḍassa issaro  
  
       tato aṅgasatā turā  parivārenti maṃ sadā  
 anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ  
 mātukucchigatassāpi vajjare bheriyo sadā  
  
       upaṭṭhahitvā  sambuddhaṃ anubhotvāna  sampadā  
 sivaṃ sukhemaṃ amataṃ pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
    yassāyaṃ īdisā  machasaṃ  yassāyamedisā  sī  mu  
    pūjaniyo  syā  sīmu  machasaṃ  
    upaṭṭhahaṃ  sī  
    turiyā  machasaṃ 
    upaṭṭhitvāna  machasaṃ  
    anubhutvāna  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekasaṅkhiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 ekasaṅkhiyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ  
  
     pāṭihīrasaññakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       padumuttaro              nāma jino āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 vasīsatasahassehi nagaraṃ pāvisī tadā  
  
       nagaraṃ pavisantassa upasantassa tādino  
 ratanāni pajjotiṃsu  nigghoso āsi tāvade  
  
       buddhassa anubhāvena bherī vajjumaghaṭṭitā  
 sayaṃ vīṇā pavajjanti buddhassa visato  puraṃ  
  
       buddhaseṭṭhaṃ na passāmi  padumuttaraṃ mahāmuniṃ  
 pāṭihīraṃ ca passitvā tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
  
       aho buddho aho dhammo aho no satthusampadā  
 acetanāpi turiyā sayameva pavajjare  
  
       satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgoma bandhanaṃ chetvā vihārāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
       paṭismabhidā catasso ca vimokkhopi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pāṭihīrasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 pāṭihīrasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ  
  
    panādiṃsu      
    pacisato  machasaṃ  
    namassāmi  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
      ñāṇatthavikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       kaṇikāraṃva jalitaṃ dīparukkhaṃva jotitaṃ  
 kañcanaṃva virocannaṃ addasaṃ dipaduttamaṃ  
  
       kamaṇḍaluṃ phapetvāna vākacīraṃ ca kuṇḍikaṃ  
 ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā buddhaseṭṭhaṃ thaviṃ ahaṃ  
  
       tamandhakāraṃ vidhamaṃ mohajālasamākulaṃ  
 ñāṇālokaṃ dassayitvā  nittiṇṇosi mahāmuni  
  
       samuddharasimaṃ lokaṃ sabbāvantamanuttara   
 ñāṇe te upamā natthi yāvatā jagato gati    
  
       tena ñāṇena sabbaññu iti buddho pavuccati  
 vandāmi taṃ mahāvīra sabbaññutamanāvaraṃ  
  
       satasahasse              ito  kappe buddhaseṭṭhaṃ thaviṃ ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ñāṇatthavāyidaṃ  phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ñāṇatthaviko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 ñāṇatthavikattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ  
  
      ucchukhaṇḍikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       nagare bandhumatiyā dvārapālo abhosahaṃ  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ  
  
       uccukhaṇḍakamādāya buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano vipassissa mahesino  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ ucchumadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhājānāmi ucchukhaṇḍassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
    dassetvāna  machasaṃ  
    anuttaraṃ  sabbattha  
    yāvatā ca gatogati      
    satasahassito  machasaṃ  
    ñāṇathavanāyidaṃ  sīmu  
  
               
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ucchukaṇḍiko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 ucchukhaṇḍikattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ  
  
     kalambadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
                    romaso nāma sambuddho vasanī pabbatantare  
 kalambaṃ tassa pādāsiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi 
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kalambassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kalambadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 kalambakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ  
  
      ambāṭakadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       vipine buddhaṃ disvāna sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ  
 ambāṭakaṃ gahetvāna sayambhussa adāsahaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
               
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambāṭakadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 ambāṭakadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ  
  
      harītakadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       harītakaṃ āmalakaṃ ambajambu vibhitakaṃ  
 kolaṃ bhallātakaṃ billaṃ sayamevāharāmahaṃ  
  
       disvāna pabbhāragataṃ jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ muniṃ  
 ābādhena papīḷentaṃ  adutiyaṃ mahāmuniṃ  
  
       harītakaṃ gahetvāna sayambhussa adāsahaṃ  
 katamattambhi  bhesajje vyādhi passambhi tāvade  
  
       pahīnadaratho buddho anumodanīyaṃ akā   
 bhesajjadāneniminā vyādhivūpasamena ca  
  
       devabhūto manusso vā jāto vā aññajātiyā  
 sabbattha sukhito hohi  mā ca te vyādhi āgamā    
  
       idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho sayambhu aparājito  
 nabhaṃ abbhuggami dhīro haṃsarājāva ambare  
  
       yato harīṭakamadaṃ  sayambhussa mahesino  
 imaṃ jātimupādāya vyādhi me nupajjatha  
  
       ayaṃ pacchimako mayhaṃ carimo vattate bhavo  
 tisso vijjā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
    āpīḷentaṃ  machasaṃ  
    khādamattamhi  machasaṃ  
    anumodamakāsi me  machasaṃ  
    hotu  machasaṃ  
    byādhimāgamā  machasaṃ  
    harītakaṃ dinnaṃ  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       catunavute ito kappe bhesajjamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhesajjassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā              jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchakatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā harītakadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 harītakadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ  
  
      ambapiṇḍiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       hatthirājā tadā āsiṃ īsādanto urūḷhavā  
 vivaranto brahāraññe addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
  
       ambapiṇḍiṃ  gahetvāna adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ  
 paṭigaṇhi mahāvīro siddhattho lokanāyako  
  
       mama nijjhāyamānassa paribhuñji tadā jino  
 tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ  
  
       tato ahaṃ cavitvāna cakkavatti ahosahaṃ  
 eteneva upāyena anubhotvāna sampadā  
  
       padhānapahitattohaṃ upasanto nirūpadhi  
 sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
    ambapīṇḍaṃ  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambapiṇḍiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 ambapiṇḍiyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ  
  
      jambuphaliyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       padumuttarabuddhassa lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  
 piṇḍāya vivarantassa dhāreto  uttamaṃ yasaṃ  
  
       aggaphalaṃ gahetvāna vippasantena cetasā  
 dakkhiṇeyyassa vīrassa adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ  
  
       tena kammena dipadinda  lokajeṭṭha narāsabha  
 pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ hitvā jayaparājayaṃ  
  
       satasahasse              ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi aggadādanassīdaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgo ca bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā jambuphaliyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 jambuphaliyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ  
  
 uddānaṃ  
  
 thero ekavihārī ca saṅkhiko  pāṭihīrako  
 thaviko ucchukhaṇḍi ca kalambambāṭakappadā   
 harītakambapiṇḍi ca jambudo  dasamo sati  chaḷāsīti ca gāthāyo gaṇitāyo vibhāvīhi  
  
 ekavihārivaggo catuttāḷisamo  
  
    dhārato  machasaṃ  
    dvipadinda  machasaṃ  
    saṅkhiyo  machasaṃ  
    kalambaambāṭakado  machasaṃ  
    ambado  machasaṃ  
   ambaphaliyatthera apadānaṃ  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
      vibhīṭakamiñjiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       kakusandho mahāvīro sabbadhammānapāragū  
 gaṇamhā vūpakaṭṭho so agamāsi vanantaraṃ  
  
       bījamiñjaṃ gahetvāna latāya āvuṇiṃ ahaṃ  
 bhagavā tamhi samaye jhāyate pabbatantare  
  
       disvānahaṃ devadevaṃ vippasannena cetasā  
 dakkhiṇeyyassa vīrassa bījamiñjamadāsahaṃ 
  
       imasmiññeva kappasmiṃ  yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ  tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bījamiñjassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vibhiṭakamiñjiyo  thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 vibhiṭakamiñjiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ  
  
     koladāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       ajinena              nivatthehaṃ vākavīradharo tadā  
 khāribhāraṃ haritvāna  kolamāharimassamaṃ    
  
       tamhi kāle sikhī buddho eko adutiyo ahu  
 mamassamamupāgañchi  jānanto sabbakālikaṃ  
  
       sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā vanditvāna ca subbataṃ  
 ubho hatthehi paggayha kolaṃ buddhassadāsahaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi koladānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
    kappamhi  machasaṃ  
    miñjamadadiṃ  machasaṃ  bījamadadiṃ  syā  
    vibhitakamiñjiyo  machasaṃ  
    khāriyā pūrayitvāna  machasaṃ  
    kolaṃhāsiṃ mamassamaṃ  machasaṃ  
    mamassamamupāgacchi  sīmu  
  
               
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā koladāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 koladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ  
  
      billaphaliyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       candabhāgānadītīre assamo sukato mama  
 billarukkhehi  ākiṇṇo nānādumanisevito  
  
       sugandhaṃ beluvaṃ disvā buddhaseṭṭhamanussariṃ  
 khāribhāraṃ pūrayitvā tuṭṭho saṃviggamānaso  
  
       kakusandhaṃ upāgamma billapakkamadāsahaṃ  
 puññakkhettassa vīrassa vippasannena cetasā  
  
       imasmiṃ yeva kappasmiṃ yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ  tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā billaphaliyatthero thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 billaphaliyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ  
  
    belurukkhehi  sīmu  beluvarukkhehi  syā  
    yaṃ phalamadadiṃ  machasaṃ  
   bilaliyatthera apadāna  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
      bhallātakadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ              sambuddhaṃ khattiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ  
 pavanaggena  gacchantaṃ sālarājaṃva phullitaṃ 
  
       tiṇattharaṃ paññapetvā buddhaseṭṭhamayācahaṃ  
 anukampatu maṃ buddho bhikkhamicchāmi dātave  
  
       anukampako kāruṇiko atthadassī mahāyaso  
 mama saṅkappamaññāya oruhī mama assame  
  
       oruhitvāna  sambuddho nisīdi paṇṇasanthare  
 bhallātakaṃ gahetvāna buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ  
  
       mama nijjhāyamānassa paribhuñji tadā jino  
 tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā abhivandiṃ tadā jinaṃ  
  
       aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 bhallātakadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā koladāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
      uttalipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       nigrodhe haritobhāse saṃvirūḷhamhi pādape  
 uttalimālaṃ  paggayha bodhiyā abhiropayiṃ  
  
       imasmiṃ yeva kappamhi yaṃ pupphambhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bodhipūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
    vipinaggena  machasaṃ  
    oruyahitvāna  sīmu  orohitvāna  machasaṃ  
    ummāmālaṃ hi  syā  
   bhallātadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uttalipupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 uttalipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ  
  
      ambāṭakiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       supupphitaṃ              sālavanaṃ ogayha vessabhu muni  
 nisīdi giriduggesu abhijātova kesarī  
  
       pasannacitto sumano ambāṭakamapūjayiṃ  
 puññakkhettaṃ mahāvīraṃ  pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphambhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambāṭakiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 ambāṭakiyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ  
  
      sīhāsanikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       padumuttarassa bhagavato sabbabhūtahitesino  
 pasannacitto sumano sīhāsanamadāsahaṃ  
  
       devaloke manusse vā yattha yattha vasāmahaṃ  
 labhāmi vipulaṃ vyamhaṃ sīhāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
    anuttaraṃ  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       soṇṇamayā rūpimayā lohitaṅkamayā  bahū  
 maṇimayā ca pallaṅkā nibbattanti mamaṃ sadā  
  
       bodhiyā āsanaṃ katvā jalajuttamanāmino  
 ucce kule pajāyāmi aho dhammasudhammatā  
  
       satasahasse ito kappe sīhāsanamakāsahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sīhāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sīhāsaniko thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 sīhāsanikattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ  
  
      pādapīṭhiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       sumedho              nāma sambuddho aggo kāruṇiko muni  
 tārayitvā bahū satte nibbuto so mahāyaso  
  
       sīhāsanassa sāmantā sumedhassa mahesino  
 pasannacitto sumano pādapīṭhamakārayiṃ  
  
       katvāna kusalaṃ sukhapākaṃ sukhudrayaṃ  
 puññakammena saṃyutto tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ  
  
       tattha me vasamānassa puññakammasamaṅgino  
 padāni uddhārantassa soṇṇapīṭhā bhavanti me  
  
       lābhā tesaṃ suladdhaṃ vo ye labhanti upassutiṃ  
 nibbute kāraṃ katvāna labhanti vipulaṃ sukhaṃ  
  
    lohitaṅgamayā  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       mayāpi sukataṃ kammaṃ vāṇijjaṃ suppayojitaṃ  
 pādapīṭhaṃ karitvāna soṇṇapīṭhaṃ labhāmahaṃ  
  
       yaṃ yaṃ disaṃ pakkamāmi kenaci paccayenahaṃ    
 soṇṇapīṭhe akkamāmi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       tiṃsakappasahassambhi yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pādapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pādapīṭhiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 pādapīṭhīyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ  
  
      vedikārakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       padumuttarabuddhassa  bodhiyā pādaputtame  
 vedikaṃ sukataṃ katvā sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
  
       atoḷārāni  bhaṇḍāni katāni akatāni ca  
 antaḷikkhā pavassanti vedikāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ubhato vyuḷhasaṅgāme pakkhandanto bhayānake  
 bhayabheravaṃ na passāmi vedikāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       mama              saṅkappamaññāya vyambhaṃ nibbattate subhaṃ  
 sayanāni mahagghāni vedikāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       satasahasso ito kappe yaṃ vedikamakārayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vedikāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
    kiccayenahaṃ  machasaṃ  
    padumuttarassa bhagavato  machasaṃ  
    athoḷārāni  sīmu  aggoḷārāni  syā  
               
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vedikārako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 vedikārakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ  
  
      bodhighariyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       siddhatthassa bhagavato dipadindassa tādino  
 pasannacitto sumano bodhigharamakārayiṃ  
  
       tusitaṃ upapannomhi vasāmi ratane ghare  
 na me sītaṃ vā uṇhaṃ vā vāto gatte na samaphuse  
  
       pañcasaṭṭhimhito kappe cakkavatti ahosahaṃ  
 kāyikaṃ nāma nagaraṃ vissakammena  māpitaṃ  
  
       dasayojanaāyāmaṃ aṭṭhayojanavitthataṃ  
 na tamhi nagare atthi kaṭṭhaṃ vallī ca mattikā  
  
       tiriyaṃ yojanaṃ āsi aḍḍhayojanacitthato    
 maṅgalo nāma pāsādo vissakammena māpito  
  
       cullāsītisahassāni thamhā soṇṇamayā ahuṃ  
 maṇimayā ca niyyuhā chadanaṃ rūpiyaṃ ahu  
  
       sabbasoṇṇamayaṃ gharaṃ vissakammena māpitaṃ  
 ajjhāvutthaṃ mayā etaṃ gharadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       te sabbe anubhotvāna devamānusake bhave  
 ajja pattomhi nibbānaṃ santipadamanuttaraṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe  bodhigharamakārayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi gharadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
    visukammena  syā  
    addhayojanacitthataṃ  machasaṃ  
    tiṃsakappasahassamhi  machasaṃ  
   bodhigharadāyakattherāpadāna  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       paṭisambhidā              catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bodhighariyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 bodhighariyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ  
  
 vibhīṭakavaggo pañcacattāḷisamo  
  
 uddānaṃ  
  
 viṭabhīkī kolaphalī billa bhallātakappadā  
 uttalambāṭakī  ceva āsanī pādapīṭhako  
 vediko bodhighariko gāthāyo gaṇitā viha  
 ekūnāsītikā sabbā asmiṃ vagge sakittitā  
  
      jatatidāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       dhammadassissa munino bodhiyā pādaputtame  
 pasannacitto sumano jagatiṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       darito pabbatāto vā  rukkhoto patito ahaṃ  
 cuto patiṭṭhaṃ vindāmi jagatiyā idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       na me corā pasahanti  nātimaññeti khattiyo    
 sabbāmittetikkamāmi jagatiyā idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ  
 sabbattha pūjato homi jagatiyā idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       aṭṭhārase kappasate jagatiṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi jagatidānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā jagatidāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 jagatidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ  
  
    billabhallātakappado  machasaṃ  
    nigrodhambāṭakī  sīmu 
    darito pabbatato vā  machasaṃ  
    vibhesanti  machasaṃ  
   nātimaññanti khantiyā  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
      morahatthiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       morahatthaṃ              gahetvāna upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano morahatthamadāsahaṃ  
  
       iminā morahatthena cetanā paṇīdhīhi ca  
 nibbāyiṃsu tayo aggī labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ  
  
       aho buddhā  aho dhammā  aho no satthusampadā  
 datvānahaṃ morahatthaṃ labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ  
  
       tiyaggī  nibbutā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā natthidāni punabbhavo  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi morahatthassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā morahatthiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 morahatthiyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ  
  
      sīhāsanavījakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       tissassāhaṃ bhagavato bodhirukkhamavandisaṃ  
 paggayhaṃ vījaniṃ tattha sīhāsanamavījayiṃ  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe sīhāsanamavījahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vījanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
    buddho  machasaṃ  
    dhammo  machasaṃ  
    tidhagagī  syā  tivaggī      
  
               
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sīhāsanavījako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 sīhāsanavījakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ  
  
      tiukkādhārakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       padumuttarabuddhassa              bodhiyā pādaputtame  
 pasannacitto sumano tayo ukkā adhārayiṃ  
  
       satasahasse ito kappe sohaṃ ukkamadhārayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ukkādānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ

 tiukkādhārakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ  
  
      akkamanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       kakusandhassa munino brāhmaṇassa vusīvato  
 divāvihāraṃ vajato akkamanamadāsahaṃ  
  
       imasmiṃ yeva kappasmiṃ yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi akkamanassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
               
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ

 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā akkamanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 akkamanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ  
  
      vanakoraṇḍiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       siddhatthassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  
 vanakoraṇḍamādāya buddhassa abhiropayiṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphambhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vanakoraṇḍiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 vanakoraṇḍiyattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhiṃ  
  
 vīsatimaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ  
  
      ekachattiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       aṅgārajātā              paṭhavī  kukkulānugatā mahī  
 padumuttaro bhagavā abbhokāsambhi caṅkami  
  
       paṇḍaraṃ chattamādāya addhāna paṭipajjahaṃ  
 tattha disvāna sambuddhaṃ vitti me upapajjatha  
  
    pathavavī  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       marīciyotthaṭā  bhūmi aṅgārava mahī ayaṃ  
 upavāyanti  mahāvātā sarīrassāsukhepanā    
  
       sītaṃ uṇhaṃ vihanantaṃ  vātātapanivāraṇaṃ  
 paṭigaṇha imaṃ chattaṃ phassayissāmi nibbutiṃ  
  
       anukampako kāruṇiko padumuttaro mahāisi    
 mamasaṅkappamaññāya paṭigaṇhi tadā jino  
  
       tiṃsakappāni devindo devarajjamakārayiṃ  
 satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca cakkavatti sukatamattano  
  
       padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ  
 anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ pubbe sukatamattano  
  
       ayaṃ me pacchimā jāti carimo vattate bhavo  
 ajjāpi setacchattaṃ me sabbakālaṃ dharīyati  
  
       satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ chattamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi chattadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekachattiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 ekachattiyattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ  
  
      jātipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       jarinibbute bhagavati padumuttare mahāyase  
 pupphavaṭaṃsake katvā  sarīrambhiropayiṃ  
  
       tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā nimmāṇaṃ agamāsahaṃ  
 devalokagato santo puññakammaṃ sarāmahaṃ  
  
    marīcivophunā  syā  marīcivophuṭā     
    upahanti  machasaṃ  
    sarīrakāyukhopana  syā  
    vibhanti  syā 
    mahāyaso  machasaṃ  
    pupphacaṅkoṭake gahetvā  syā  
  
               
  
       ambarā              pupphavasso me sabbakālaṃ pavassati  
 saṃsarāmi manusse ce rājā homi mahāyaso  
  
       tahiṃ kusumavasso me abhivassati sabbadā  
 tasseva  pupphapūjāya vāhasā sabbadassino 
  
       ayaṃ pacchimako mayhaṃ carimo vattate bhavo  
 ajjāpi pupphavasso me abhivassati sabbadā  
  
       satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ pupphambhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dehapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā jātipupphiyo  thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 jātipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ  
  
      paṭaṭipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       nīharante sarīrambhi vajjamānāsu bherisu  
 pasannacitto sumano paṭṭipupphamapūjayiṃ  
  
       satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ pupphambhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dehapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paṭaṭipupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 paṭaṭipupphiyayattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ  
  
    kāyesu  syā tāyeva      
    sattipaṇṇiyo  syā      
  
               
  
      gandhapūjakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       citesu kayiramānesu  nānāgandhe samāhaṭe 
 pasanna citto sumano gandhamuṭṭhimapūjayiṃ  
  
       satasahasse ito kappe citakaṃ yamapūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi citapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
       paṭisambhidā              catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gandhapūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 gandhapūjakattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ  
  
 uddānaṃ  
  
 jagatī morahatthi ca āsanī ukkadhārako  
 akkamī vanakoraṇḍi chattado jātipūjako  
 paṭṭipupphī ca yo thero dasamo gandhapūjako  
 sattasaṭṭhi ca gāthāyo gaṇitāyo vibhāvihi  
  
 jagatidāyakavaggo chacattāḷīsamo  
  
      sālakusumiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       parinibbute bhagavati jalajuttamanāmake  
 āropitambhi catake sālapupphamapūjayiṃ  
  
       satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ pupphambhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi citapūjāyidaṃ  phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
    citāsu kurumānāsu  machasaṃ  
    buddhapūjāyidā  syā  
  
               
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sālakusumiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhisitthāti  
  
 sālakusumiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ  
  
      citakapūjakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       jhāyamānassa bhagavato sikhino lokabandhuno  
 aṭṭhacampakapupphāni citakaṃ abhiropayiṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphambhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi citakapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo

 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ

 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā citakapūjako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 citakapūjakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ  
  
      citakanibbāpakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       dayhamāne              sarīrambhi vessabhussa mahesino  
 gandhodakaṃ gahetvāna citaṃ nibbāpayiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe citaṃ nibbāpayiṃ ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi gandhodakassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo

 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā citakanibbāpako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
  
 citakanibbāpakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ  
  
      setudāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       vipassino bhagavato caṅkamantassa sammukhā  
 pasannacitto sumano setuṃ kārāpayiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ setuṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo

 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ
